In the Tyrant’s World.

Song Shuhang’s main body remained in a state of closed-door cultivation. The spiritual energy within him surged and exploded. When he was at the Eighth Stage Realm, his physique, spiritual energy, and primordial spirit had already surpassed those of ordinary Tribulation Transcenders. But now, even his realm had to be forcefully broken through using the ‘Three Separations’ secret technique.

Above his head, Pavilion Master Chu was in an excellent mood, occasionally transforming her hair into various shapes: triangles, quadrilaterals, pentagrams... and even heart shapes.

Not far away, Immortal Fairy White Bones was also in high spirits. She glanced at Song Shuhang from time to time and began the “simulation training three years later” in her heart.

Compared to the White Dragon and Pavilion Master Chu, she had a significant advantage—she didn’t have any ‘juniors’ hanging around Tyrannical Song!

The White Dragon had Su Clan’s Sixteen, and this little fairy had a very deep relationship with Tyrannical Song.

Pavilion Master Chu had the ghost spirit fairy, and if the ghost spirit fairy was attached to Song Shuhang’s body, it was equivalent to Tyrannical Song. Even Pavilion Master Chu herself was an accessory to Tyrannical Song.

Their ‘juniors’ were all of the same generation as Tyrannical Song, so if they wanted to call him ‘Daddy’ in the future, there would be an additional layer of mental barrier.

It was even possible that their ‘juniors’ were candidates for their mothers.

As for her, Immortal Fairy White Bones, she had nothing to worry about!

Therefore, it was better for the two sisters to continue being her close sisters or elder aunts. She could take care of the triplets in the future. In fact, she didn’t even mind calling them Grandma White Dragon or Grandma Chu in the future.

Immortal Fairy White Bones was delighted.

She secretly glanced at Tyrannical Song again, finding him more and more pleasing to the eye... After all, he was going to be a father in the future.

Opposite Song Shuhang.

The ghost spirit fairy bowed to Pavilion Master Chu and said, “Pavilion Master, it’s about time. Shuhang’s realm has almost reached its limit. Next, I’ll give Shuhang’s ‘self corpse’ time to complete the ritual of severing three corpses.”

“Go. Remember to show up occasionally. Don’t be invisible like before,” Pavilion Master Chu replied in a lazy voice.

“Yes, I will,” the ghost fairy giggled.

After saying that, she gently tapped her glabella and pressed the ‘switch’ again.

Then, her state became transparent and gradually disappeared from everyone’s memories...

When the ghost fairy turned transparent, the presence of Tyrannical Song’s third corpse, the Self-centric Corpse, appeared in front of everyone.

The third corpse still maintained its outstretched hand, and Zither Master Fengyi’s claws were standing on his arm. The Self-centric Corpse had inherited Tyrannical Song’s true gentleness, and every move it made was extremely warm.

“Eh? Has he appeared?” Zither Master Fengyi said with her claws.

“The communication with the ghost spirit fairy has ended, so she left her presence to me,” the Self-centric Corpse smiled. He stretched out his hand and placed Zither Master Fengyi’s claw on his shoulder.

Then, he stepped down from the lotus platform.

When he stepped down, the lotus platform instantly turned into countless specks of light and dissipated.

The Self-centric Corpse stepped into the air and walked toward Tyrannical Song’s main body. Beneath his feet, lotuses blossomed with every step. Unlike the black lotus on Song Shuhang’s main body, the lotus under the self corpse’s feet was pure white.

After arriving in front of his main body, the Self-centric Corpse bowed to Tyrannical Song’s main body and called out, “Overlord Body, I’m here to greet you.”

This was the final ritual of the Three Separations Secret Technique.

It was just that Tyrannical Song’s main body was a shell that had lost its soul. Tyrannical Song’s primordial spirit projection was still lingering in the Heavenly Dao Prison World. Therefore, this shell couldn’t respond to the third corpse.

Fortunately, Tyrannical Song had many accessories on him.

The virtuous lamia wasn’t around, so Black Panther didn’t know much about the ritual of ‘Three Separations.’

Therefore, it was Fairy Creation’s turn to appear.

Fairy Creation coughed lightly. She then entered Song Shuhang’s body and said in his voice, “Fellow Daoist, there’s no need to be so polite. We are one.”

Imitating a voice was a piece of cake for a song immortal like Fairy Creation.

This voice came from Song Shuhang’s body, and it could barely be considered as completing the etiquette.

Opposite her, the Self-centric Corpse Overlord Body looked at Fairy Creation gratefully.

“From now on, the three corpses will return to their original positions,” Overlord Body said slowly.

Following his announcement, Song Shuhang’s realm broke through!

The Tribulation Transcender’s life force, the spatial tribulation bone, and the primordial spirit that was entrusted to the Tribulation Transcender’s void resonated at the same time.

The special effect of the Three Separations Slaying Secret Technique allowed Song Shuhang to forcefully advance to the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm without transcending the tribulation.

The Tribulation Transcender’s life force erupted, extending Song Shuhang’s life force indefinitely.

The complete Space Calamity Bone grew inside Tyrannical Song’s body. It was so huge that it wasn’t just a section, but it covered Tyrannical Song’s entire body, turning all his bones into it.

The primordial spirit that was placed in the void of the Tribulation Transcender was strengthened once again. Each of the 15+1 primordial spirits was nourished and strengthened. This was the nourishment and strengthening of the Tribulation Transcender’s primordial spirit that was 15+1 times stronger!

Walla

Spatial fluctuations appeared.

Song Shuhang’s primordial spirit, which was in the Wielder’s small black room, was sent back. At the same time, Fairy Virtuous returned with the ‘Good Corpse Spear’ in her hand.

A wisp of Father Goudan’s consciousness and a wisp of Senior Three-Eyed’s consciousness... They were still in the Wielder of the Will’s small black room, loving and killing each other.

After Song Shuhang’s primordial spirit projection returned to its original position, his main body opened its eyes.

“I’m finally back... I almost thought that I was going to retire in the Heavenly Dao Prison World,” Song Shuhang said slowly.

After his primordial spirit returned, he stretched out his hand and tapped lightly.

In the shadow, the inner demon appeared and transformed into the Evil Corpse, Ba E.

The virtuous lamia rode on the whale and waved the Good Corpse-Bashan in her hand.

Self-centric Corpse Overlord Body stood in the center.

The spiritual energy in Song Shuhang’s main body surged crazily.

Immortal Fairy White Bones, Pavilion Master Chu, Golden Trigram, Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, Zither Master Phoenix Rites, and the other Immortals all sensed something and looked at Song Shuhang.

They could clearly feel that the ‘path to immortality’ on Song Shuhang’s body had become clearer...

In other words, Song Shuhang had already condensed the embryonic form of his own ‘path to immortality’? Stepping into the realm of a top-notch Tribulation Transcender in one step?

“Pavilion Master Chu, Fairy Creation, Black Panther, wait for me in the Tyrant’s Realm. I’ll be right back,” Song Shuhang said.

“Tribulation?” Pavilion Master Chu asked in a daze.

“Yes, I’m going to see the Tribulation Transcender’s Thousand-Day Tribulation,” Song Shuhang nodded.

After saying that, he stretched out his hand and pressed down in the air. He activated the power of space, and the lotus of virtue that he had promised Scholar Yukong was transferred over.

This lotus flower of virtue that had the effect of ‘avoiding tribulation,’ along with the effect of Song Shuhang’s ghost spirit fairy’s “Forgotten Divine Technique,” had finally completed the last part of Song Shuhang’s heavenly tribulation.

“Tyrannical Song, how long will it take?” Fairy Creation sang.

“I’ll be right back!” Song Shuhang replied handsomely.

The next moment, he stood up and took a step forward.

With one step, he stepped into the space of the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation.

“Senior Melon Eater, I’m here to take over the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage.”

Chapter 2852: You Don’t Even Qualify to Make Me Use the Hezhu Pillar!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

This time, Song Shuhang entered the space of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation using his own abilities!

In the beginning, he had come in thanks to Senior Melon Eater’s Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation. Then, under the control of Ma’am Long Luo and Senior White, he had entered and exited the space of a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender.

Although relying on Lady Long Luo and Senior White to bully the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation was fun, doing it with his own abilities would indeed give him a greater sense of accomplishment!

At this moment, in the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation Realm.

The Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation that originally belonged to Sage Monarch Melon Eater was now divided into two worlds, east and west.

The members who were transcending the tribulation were separated and could not take care of each other.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater was all alone, struggling to support one world as he endured his thousand-day tribulation.

On the other side, Song Shuhang’s clone and Senior White’s half-body and half-clone combination were also going through their thousand-day tribulation.

In the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation Realm, the power of the heavenly tribulation would become stronger with each passing day. Now that more than three months had passed, the power of the Thousand Day Tribulation had already reached +100.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater had already transformed into his virtuous divine whale body, struggling to hold on. He opened up the ‘network of virtue’ around him and had to burn his lifespan from time to time to support it. When ordinary Profound Sages transcended a Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation, they would have to burn their lifespan to unleash their power.

Therefore, when an Eighth Stage Profound Sage tried to break through to the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm, the younger, the better. The longer the lifespan, the more confident he would be.

As long as he advanced to the Tribulation Transcender Realm, his lifespan would be greatly extended. Tribulation Transcenders had long lifespans. As long as they didn’t seek death, there weren’t many Tribulation Transcenders who died of old age.

At the same time, Sage Monarch Melon Eater would pay attention to Song Shuhang and Sage White from time to time, hoping that they could hold on.

Song Shuhang and Senior White had been accidentally dragged into his Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation, and he felt very guilty. If the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation Realm hadn’t been separated into two spaces, he would have done his best to help Song Shuhang and Sage White. Sage Monarch Melon Eater, who could condense a large amount of merit, was very kind.

The three of them transcending the tribulation as a group strengthened the effect of the heavenly tribulation to a certain extent. However, splitting the heavenly tribulation into two meant that Song Shuhang and Sage White shared half of the power of the heavenly tribulation with Sage Monarch Melon Eater.

Therefore, in theory, as long as Song Shuhang and Sage White were able to hold on, the power of Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation would decrease.

Therefore, no matter what, Sage Monarch Melon Eater hoped that Song Shuhang and Sage White could persevere and survive the remaining 900 days of the heavenly tribulation.

“All the best, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song. We can do it. We’ve already transcended one-tenth of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation.” Sage Monarch Melon Eater narrowed his eyes as he looked at Song Shuhang and Sage White, who were on the other side. He was silently cheering for them.

Just as Sage Monarch Melon Eater was silently cheering for Tyrannical Song... Suddenly, there was a strange movement in the Heavenly Tribulation Space on the other side!

Intense spatial fluctuations were produced.

Someone had forcefully torn apart the space of the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation and entered the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation!

“Again?” Sage Monarch Melon Eater was anxious.

What happened to little friend Tyrannical Song?

Three months ago, all kinds of situations kept happening at little friend Tyrannical Song’s place, and he even sent a few guests in, almost killing them several times... Would something similar happen again this time?

“Hahaha, I’m finally here. As expected, we will still enter this Heavenly Tribulation Realm...It won’t reopen a new Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation space.” Another Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s voice sounded.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater turned his eyes and saw a taller and older ‘Tyrannical Song,’ stepping on a black lotus.

This is little friend Tyrannical Song’s true body?

Song Shuhang’s gaze also fell on his clone.

Three months ago, the clone that he had used to replace himself with Ma’am Long Luo and Senior White seemed to be a little shorter than his current body. Even her face looked a little more tender...

This kind of tenderness did not only refer to appearance, but also in terms of spiritual temperament.

[That’s true. I’ve experienced many things in the past three months.] Song Shuhang thought to himself.

The clone had been transcending the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation in place of the main body, so its temperament had not changed much. However, his main body had advanced from the Sixth Stage to the current Ninth Stage in one go. It had risen by three major realms, so his temperament would naturally be a little more ancient.

He didn’t pay attention to her height. Now, it seemed that his height had increased by another notch...

“Fellow Daoist, you’ve worked hard.” Song Shuhang said to his clone.

This clone was different from the ‘Three Separations’ clone. It didn’t have its own consciousness and was completely controlled by Song Shuhang. Previously, when he was in the Tribulation Transcendence Space, he also relied on a wisp of divine sense to operate.

Now that the main body had returned, the clone smiled and turned into a cloud of smoke with a bang, merging into the main body. At the same time, his experiences of transcending the tribulation in the past three months were also integrated into Song Shuhang’s memories.

“Senior White ~ you’ve worked hard too.” Song Shuhang said to Senior White.

Senior White waved his upper body and replied,” Stop fooling around. I was just cut up and sent here. How could it be hard?”

“Senior White, let’s end this thousand-day tribulation together!” Song Shuhang said seriously.

“Yes.” Senior White’s clone replied, “I hope to return before the new year.”

“Senior White, your wish is our goal.” Song Shuhang said handsomely.

Then, he shouted at Sage Monarch Melon Eater from afar, “Senior Melon Eater, are you alright? Can you still hold on? I’m here to take over the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage ~”

Sage Monarch Melon Eater: “Little friend Tyrannical Song, be careful!”

He saw that after Tyrannical Song came in, the power of the heavenly tribulation on the other side had increased dramatically. In fact, half of the power of the heavenly tribulation on his side had been drawn away.

In the space of the heavenly tribulation on the other side, the power of the heavenly tribulation had transformed into a huge bow. On it, the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning, which was specially aimed at ‘geniuses of heavens,’ had transformed into an arrow and was aimed at Song Shuhang.

Nearly a thousand Nine Heavens Divine Thunderbolts, which were specially targeted at the geniuses who had the ability to fight across levels, were highly compressed and turned into destructive arrows.

As soon as the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow took shape, it gave Sage Monarch Melon Eater a huge sense of oppression. Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s soul seemed to be trembling.

If this arrow went down, even a heaven’s favored son who could fight across levels would die on the spot, right?

Can little friend Tyrannical Song block this arrow?

“Yo, this is interesting.” Song Shuhang looked at the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow in the sky and said in a relaxed manner.

Unknowingly...This heavenly tribulation that could kill Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcenders actually didn’t give him any pressure.

“Although it doesn’t feel too painful to be shot, I ‘M not a masochist after all. I don’t have the hobby of being blown up while standing.” Song Shuhang said softly.

“Come out, Longevity Pillar. Kun King Pillar!” he said.

Facing such a powerful heavenly tribulation, he didn’t even need to use the Hezhu Pillar!

Chapter 2853: The Charm of Heavenly Tribulations, Discounts Available Online

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Additionally, the Longevity Pillar, Kun King Pillar, had a very practical skill, Black Hole Devour. This skill could directly devour the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow and preserve it.

After all, King Kun inherently had the attribute of devouring everything, and there was an incomparably huge small world within his body.

Boom

In the sky, the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow, with the power to destroy the world, shot toward Song Shuhang and Senior White.

When the arrow of divine lightning was shot out, space itself was shattered!

In an instant, the Heavenly Lightning Divine Arrow pierced through space and directly appeared above Song Shuhang’s head, fiercely exploding!

In the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage, the heavenly lightning actually contained the power of space. This was a very cheating matter.

Unfortunately, even with the addition of the strange spatial power, this Heavenly Thunder God Arrow was destined to be unable to establish any effect.

The body of the Longevity Pillar, Kun King Pillar, directly turned into a black hole beside Song Shuhang. The lightning arrow, which was enough to kill a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender, or at least seriously injure a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender, fell into this black hole like a clay ox entering the sea... It was completely devoured by the black hole without causing any waves!

Not to mention the waves, there was not even a sound!

At the very least, one could hear a sound when the clay ox was thrown into the black hole. However, the Heavenly Thunder God Arrow did not even make a sound before it was humbly absorbed by the black hole!

Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s mouth was wide open, and he was so shocked that he couldn’t close his mouth. My god, he dealt with the Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow so easily?

What is the origin of little friend Song Shuhang’s pillar?

What level of magic treasure was this?

Even an ordinary Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender magical treasure wouldn’t be able to do this, right?

Could it be an Immortal’s magical treasure?

Was it because Tyrannical Song had obtained this top-grade magical treasure and had the confidence to resist the Ninth Stage Heavenly Tribulation that he returned to the Heavenly Tribulation Realm?

But that didn’t seem right. If it was an Immortal’s magical treasure, refining it would take an extremely long time. Three months wasn’t enough for Tyrannical Song to refine the Immortal magical treasure and even bring it into the heavenly tribulation, right?

Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s mind was in turmoil, and he felt like he was dreaming.

“I’ve successfully preserved this heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage. I haven’t eaten a heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage yet.” Perhaps it was because he had used up a lot of energy during the Three Separations Execution, Song Shuhang felt a long-lost sense of hunger. Just thinking about the delicacy of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation made him salivate involuntarily.

How should he eat this fresh heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage to be healthier?

Steamed? Stir-fried? Fried? Or cut it into pieces and eat it raw?

Thinking of this, Song Shuhang couldn’t control himself and greedily looked at the tribulation cloud above his head.

Come on, continue your performance, Lord Heavenly Tribulation!

This might very well be the last time we meet. After transcending the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage, theoretically, there should be no more heavenly tribulation to transcend.

Therefore, you don’t have to be polite, Lord Heavenly Tribulation. Just use whatever you have.

This is your last chance to destroy me ~

“Shuhang, be careful. The power of the heavenly tribulation on my side has decreased by another 30%. The power of the heavenly tribulation has been attracted to you!” At this time, Sage Monarch Melon Eater suddenly felt something and immediately reminded him.

He felt as if he had been underestimated by the Heavenly Tribulation...Or rather, the heavenly tribulation instinctively didn’t want to waste more energy on him. As a result, a large amount of heavenly tribulation energy was transferred to Song Shuhang’s side. They wanted to focus their fire on him first.

“Does your magic tool have a limit? You have to be careful. There might be more than one Nine Heavens Divine Lightning Arrow in the next wave.” Sage Monarch Melon Eater shouted.

He didn’t want Tyrannical Song to get into an accident because of his carelessness.

Tyrannical Song had done him a great favor, and if something happened to him during the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation, Sage Monarch Melon Eater would definitely feel extremely guilty.

“Senior Melon Eater, don’t panic!” Song Shuhang comforted him. “No matter if he wants to shoot two or three arrows, even if it’s more arrows, they won’t hurt me.”

In order to prevent Sage Monarch Melon Eater from worrying, Song Shuhang waved his hand with a smile.

Rustle

Several Overlord God Pillars rose from the ground and filled the space beside Song Shuhang.

The Longevity Pillar series consisted of the Emperor Destruction Pillar, the Void Sun Pillar, the Beyond Pillar, and the Kun King Pillar.

Merit Pillar Series: Pipi Snake Immortal Pillar.

The heavenly tribulation pillar series was an archaic pillar, a special pillar condensed from the demonic tribulation of Song Shuhang of the Netherworld.

As for the strongest pillar at the moment, the Dao Pillar, Star Dragon Pillar—a double-section pole made from the raw materials of Lady Long Luo and the clone of the big-eyed planet big shot.

A series of powerful pillars almost blinded Sage Monarch Melon Eater!

Each of these pillars had the power to destroy the world. At this time, they gathered around Tyrannical Song and vaguely set up a pillar array!

“Wherever the Overlord Divine Pillar is inserted, it is my country!” The virtuous lamia appeared behind Song Shuhang and, without hesitation, snatched the lines that belonged to Demon Emperor More than One.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater:

He thought that Tyrannical Song had only obtained one pillar, but he didn’t expect that Tyrannical Song would have so many.

If each of these pillars had the power of the Kun King Pillar, then the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage wouldn’t be able to do anything to Tyrannical Song, right?

What had Tyrannical Song’s main body experienced in the outside world during these three months? He had actually obtained such a huge opportunity and so many magic tool pillars?

As he pondered, Sage Monarch Melon Eater finally found some time to focus his attention on Tyrannical Song’s main body.

A moment later...

Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s jaw was dislocated.

Not to mention the Sage Names that started with the word tyrann, the Eight Tyrants were simply unprecedented.

Let’s first talk about Tyrannical Song’s current realm—Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender!

Melon Eater wasn’t wrong. Tyrannical Song’s current realm was a genuine Tribulation Transcender.

The Tribulation Transcender’s vitality, the Spatial Tribulation Bone, and the Primordial Spirit no longer existed in his body. Only the projection of the Primordial Spirit remained. The characteristics of the three Tribulation Transcenders had already merged into one.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater was confused.

Could it be that the world had changed and time was distorted?

I’ve been transcending the Heavenly Tribulation in the Tribulation Transcender Realm for three months, but in the outside world, 300 or 3,000 years have actually passed?

Otherwise, there was no way to explain Tyrannical Song’s current Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm, right?

Sage Monarch Melon Eater’s brain was on the verge of crashing.

However, the shock that Song Shuhang brought to him had only just begun.

“The Tyrant God Pillar Formation has been set up. The heavenly tribulation is no longer able to affect me. Then it’s time to start operating,” Song Shuhang said.

After saying that, he took out a lotus flower of virtue.

At the same time, with a thought, three figures stepped out from behind him.

Good Corpse Tyrant Good, Evil Corpse Tyrant Evil, Self Corpse Tyrant Body!

The three corpses appeared at the same time.

Song Shuhang activated the lotus flower of virtue and began to use his own methods to influence the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage above his head.

Today, he, Tyrannical Song, was going to turn the thousand-day tribulation into a ten-day tribulation!

A thousand days was too long, and Senior White was still thinking of rushing back to celebrate the new year in a few days.

Moreover, this new year was also very special to him.

This was the first New Year he had celebrated since joining the Nine Provinces Number One Group!

He didn’t want to waste such a special day in the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation space.

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation  Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“What treasure is this? I can feel an enormous amount of virtuous power from it!” Senior Melon Eater from next door couldn’t help but ask.

Currently, he had a body of virtue, and in the future, he would step out of the Great Dao of Virtue and become an existence that could attain immortality. Therefore, he was especially sensitive to treasures of the virtue system.

The moment Song Shuhang took out the golden lotus of virtue, Sage Monarch Melon Eater keenly estimated the huge amount of virtue hidden within it.

Not only that, but he could also sense a deep sense of sorrow from the golden lotus of merit.

The owner of the golden lotus of merit had performed an extremely grand deed of great merit, one that could even affect the myriad worlds, under a very sad and helpless situation. Only then had they condensed such a precious treasure of merit.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater really couldn’t imagine what kind of good deed could affect the myriad worlds, but at the same time, was accompanied by endless sadness.

Could it be that they had to destroy something they loved the most to save the myriad worlds’ merit?

“I don’t know what this Merit Golden Lotus is called either. I only know that... it can affect the heavenly tribulation,” Song Shuhang replied.

After saying that, the self-centric corpse, Overlord Body, stepped on the white lotus and pressed his hand on the golden lotus of virtue. He injected a wisp of the spirit energy of the Forgotten Divine Technique into it, activating the golden lotus of virtue.

The reason Tyrannical Song had entered the Heavenly Tribulation Realm with such confidence wasn’t because he wanted to enjoy the beating of the heavenly tribulation big shot. He had the confidence to do so, and the treasures he had collected over the past three months that could counter the heavenly tribulation were his confidence!

Walla ~~

The golden lotus of virtue bloomed, and a huge amount of light of virtue enveloped Song Shuhang and Senior White. The remaining power of the golden lotus of virtue flowed to Senior Melon Eater next door.

Everyone who saw it would have a share of the good fortune. This was also the reward for Senior Melon Eater bringing Song Shuhang and Senior White to transcend the heavenly tribulation of the Ninth Stage.

Senior Melon Eater was kind-hearted, and both Song Shuhang and Senior White could see it. Therefore, Song Shuhang and Senior White were both willing to help Sage Monarch Melon Eater at the critical moment.

The blooming golden lotus of virtue transformed into a lotus imprint and floated beside Song Shuhang, Senior White, and Senior Melon Eater.

This brand began to silently influence the heavenly tribulation above their heads, compressing the duration of the heavenly tribulation. This influence was not a one-time deal but a long, continuous stream.

As long as Song Shuhang and the others were still in the Heavenly Tribulation Realm, the lotus flower of virtue would continuously influence the heavenly tribulation. From time to time, it would tease the heavenly tribulation, causing the duration of the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation to decrease by 1, 1.

“This, there’s actually such a treasure in the world!” Senior Melon Eater said in shock.

Although the -1, -1 was very weak, and it would only cool down after a while before the -1 effect was completed, it accumulated!

One had to know that the most difficult part of the Thousand Day Tribulation was the length!

Every tribulation was a variation, with endless patterns. To give Song Shuhang a fresh experience every time he transcended the tribulation, Sir Heavenly Tribulation put in a lot of effort.

Even the father of the heavenly tribulation, Divine Punishment, Song Shuhang had encountered several times.

His understanding of the heavenly tribulation had reached a level where he could write and publish his own book!

Senior White’s understanding of the heavenly tribulation was also unfathomable. He could play with the heavenly tribulation in the palm of his hand. Every time Senior White transcended the tribulation, it wasn’t him transcending it, but the heavenly tribulation transcending him.

The top experts of the two worlds combined the data of the heavenly tribulation and analyzed the power that had invaded Song Shuhang’s body.

The analysis speed instantly evolved from 3G to 5G. With a whoosh, all kinds of heavenly tribulation forces were instantly exploded, and the analysis was completed.

However, Senior White’s goal wasn’t just to analyze the information of the heavenly tribulation. Every time Senior White attacked, he would directly target the core elements of the matter.

This time was no exception.

Senior White combined the information about Song Shuhang and himself, as well as the information about the final tribulation of the Ninth Stage, and pointed at the transcendental laws of the heavenly tribulation. This was similar to the laws of the Profound Sage Speech, which were the exclusive laws of the Wielder of the Will.

In theory, these laws couldn’t be grasped by cultivators, but under Senior White’s violent analysis, they slowly appeared in front of Senior White and Song Shuhang.

Even though he had only analyzed the tip of the iceberg of the heavenly tribulation’s laws, Song Shuhang was still greatly shocked.

“Senior White, you’re simply too awesome.” Song Shuhang felt as if he had transformed into Sage Monarch Melon Eater next door. His mind was filled with the urge to shout to express his admiration for Senior White.

“Yes, I know,” Senior White replied.

Song Shuhang didn’t even need to remind him that he was too awesome.

“I mean, Senior White, your action of analyzing the heavenly tribulation laws was awesome,” Song Shuhang added.

“Oh,” Senior White replied.

‘Eh? Why did it become a one-word reply? Could it be that Senior White isn’t satisfied with my gifts?’ Song Shuhang’s heart skipped a beat.

Just as they were in deep thought, more of the heavenly tribulation laws were exposed to Song Shuhang and Senior White.

Song Shuhang felt that his head was starting to swell and ache, as if his brain had been struck by lightning. He felt a numbing pain—this was the same as when he had come into contact with the Profound Sage Speech. It was the price he had to pay for coming into contact with transcendental laws.

If it wasn’t for the fact that he often came into contact with undying information and the pseudo-undying mode, his brain might have already been unable to withstand the impact of the heavenly tribulation laws and his head blown up by the law information!

“My head hurts,” Song Shuhang said.

“Endure it and it will pass. Hold on,” Senior White’s voice rang out.

“Don’t worry, Senior White. I’m a professional when it comes to enduring pain,” Song Shuhang said confidently.

“Yes,” Senior White said.

“Tch ~ Shuhang, what’s wrong with you today? I’m busy analyzing the laws here. Don’t mess around first,” Senior White said seriously.

“Little Song Song, if you’re bored, do you want me to sing for you?” the QQ version of Liu Xingbai’s voice rang out.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

It must be because of the intense headache that caused my brain to fall into chaos.

“Stop fooling around. We’re transcending the tribulation,” Senior White reminded.

Boom, boom, boom~

The modern heavenly tribulation in its present form was still exploding, pouring its power into Song Shuhang’s body. As Senior White’s progress in analyzing the laws of the heavenly tribulation increased, Song Shuhang’s head grew bigger and bigger, and he felt dizzy.

Next door, the heavenly tribulation of the past had already reached its end. The virtuous lamia, Song Shuhang’s clone, Song Shuhang’s three corpses, and the Overlord Divine Pillar were working together to attack.

The Overlord Divine Pillar and the virtuous lamia each displayed their magical powers, and all kinds of spells and innate abilities emerged one after another.

On the other hand, Song Shuhang’s clones, evil corpses, and self-corpses were relatively lacking.

When they faced the humanoid heavenly tribulation branded by experts, they did not waste any time. They condensed their defenses and rubbed their hands together to form “Lightning Palms” of various sizes to clash with the humanoid heavenly tribulation.

Humanoid Heavenly Tribulation A: “River of the Immortal Sword~”

Tyrannical Song’s clone: “Small City-Level Lightning Palm!”

Humanoid Heavenly Tribulation B: “Fighting Transformation Great Dao Fist Technique~”

Evil Corpse: “Overlord God Pillar + Mid-Level City Lightning Palm!”

Humanoid Heavenly Tribulation C was speechless.

The C-tribulation stood on the tribulation cloud in confusion.

In the next moment, a Mid-Level Upper City-Level Lightning Palm engulfed him mercilessly.

For a time, in the past Heavenly Tribulation Space, palm lightning of various sizes continuously exploded.

Sage Monarch Melon Eater had never thought that Tyrannical Song would be able to play tricks with just his “Lightning Palm!”

Moreover... he didn’t know if it was an illusion.

The Lightning Palm of the Heavenly Tribulation exploded the Heavenly Tribulation!

He would return the favor with his own methods!

Chapter 2866: Don’t Become a Slave to Death

Song Shuhang had absolutely no intention of refining the girl inside the “mechanical core reactor” at all!

Sometimes, being too strong was a form of torture.

Its claws gently shot out, brushing past Lady Onion’s green onion.

“Dead, dead, dead,” Lady Onion shouted.

It was the Dao artifact, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber. It automatically protected its master!

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’s precious light wrapped around the enlightenment stone fragment and Lady Onion’s root, protecting her.

At the same time, another figure appeared in the void.

It was Song Shuhang’s clone that was controlling Senior Mental Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword!

Song Shuhang’s clone grabbed Scarlet Heaven Sword with one hand and forcefully entered the black hole. Then, he used his other hand to grab the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ and Lady Onion.

“Boss Song ” At this moment, Lady Onion was so moved that she almost cried.

“Aaah ~” Before she could finish feeling touched, Song Shuhang’s clone hugged her and let out a wave of miserable screams. Then, he was swallowed by the black hole along with the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber and the Mental Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword.

Song Shuhang’s clone, Mental Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword, Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, and Lady Onion were like a huge rock, forcefully blocking the hole in the black hole!

The black hole dimensional space calmed down... Song Shuhang’s clone and Lady Onion also disappeared.

Chapter 2882: Soft Feather’s Growth

The sacrifice of Lady Onion’s meat bun team’s clones might still be effective. At least, it was like a sacrifice that appeased the anger of the black hole.

Song Shuhang said, “Heavens, it seems... Lost contact? Soft Feather, I’ll reply to you later.”

Chapter 2883: I Placed My Hopes on the Future

This might be karma.

Break through defense while spending endless money.

The path of cultivation was one step at a time.

It would take a very long time to accumulate the power from the initial Tribulation Transcender realm to the peak of the Tribulation Transcender realm.

If this continued, the workload of the giant turtle of disaster would increase tenfold.

He was a man who knew how to maximize the value of everything. Whatever fell into his hands, he could make the best use of it!

Furthermore, he couldn’t afford to waste the things he shed.

Senior White’s sword qi descended!

Song Shuhang, who was in the state of “Saber Man as One,” had a huge advantage in deciphering Dao patterns.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber would take the initiative to cooperate with him and decipher the Dao patterns on the saber.

Behind him, the ghost fairy spirit and the Inner World could provide assistance to Song Shuhang.

At this moment, Song Shuhang’s brain seemed to have been blessed. The secrets of the Dao patterns on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber were continuously developed and understood by him.

Eight Dao patterns on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber had already been unsealed, and the ninth Dao pattern was slowly being released as Song Shuhang refined it.

Each of the eight Dao patterns that had been unsealed contained some techniques left behind by Wielder of the Will Goudan’s father. They were all techniques to strengthen the energy in one’s body and increase energy control.

Some strengthened the energy defense in the body. After the second stage, the power in the cultivator’s body would automatically protect the body. From protective zhen qi to protective ling power to protective immortal essence, the first Dao pattern left behind by Goudan’s father was to strengthen control in this area.

There was a way to strengthen energy attacks. As long as one followed a certain circulation technique, the energy in one’s body would be attached with the effect of a Dao pattern when it was released, and finally, the effect would exceed the limit of one’s own realm!

Using a cultivator of the Fourth Stage as an example, if this technique was used, a cultivator of the Fourth Stage could rely on his true qi, which had been sublimated to the limit, to fight head-on with the spiritual energy of a cultivator of the Fifth Stage!

If a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender were to use this method, after the “Immortal Origin of a Tribulation Transcender” in their body sublimated to the limit, they would similarly be able to produce an effect that exceeded the limits of their Immortal Origin!

Other than the enhancement of defense and attack, there was also the extreme control of the energy in his body. This was a technique to accurately use every wisp of energy in his body so that the energy in his body would not be wasted.

Each of the eight Dao patterns contained information that was targeted at the most basic energy control and strengthening of cultivators.

For other cultivators, there might be many techniques that they couldn’t use, especially for cultivators who had advanced to the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Realm or the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm. Their control over their own energy had already reached a microscopic level.

However, to Song Shuhang, the information contained in each of these eight Dao patterns was extremely precious. What Tyrannical Song lacked the most was the foundation...

Other cultivators might not have much to improve in this aspect. However, Song Shuhang still had a lot of room for improvement in this aspect!

Moreover, Song Shuhang knew that the things within these eight Dao patterns were all warm-ups.

In fact, the ninth Dao pattern might even be a warm-up segment left behind by Wielder of the Will Goudan’s father.

Only after the warm-up was completed would he be able to face the secrets of the Heavenly Dao Goudan’s father’s escape technique after gathering all nine Dao patterns.

The process of refining the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber was very stable. It progressed steadily and did not cause any accidents.

But... Song Shuhang wanted to get the information from the saber, but he couldn’t read it!

“There’s no information about the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue,” Song Shuhang said.

The information on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber regarding Lady Onion’s identity as the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue had only stopped at the moment when Lady Onion accepted the identity of the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue and obtained the inheritance of the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

“Could it be that the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue has changed midway?” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet guessed.

The number cultivation system would change a blademaster every time it changed. However, it did not mean that he could cultivate the saber to the next transformation without any worries just because he was chosen as the saber master.

The cultivation world was cruel. Even the blademaster could die in the middle of the journey.

This was especially true for cultivators who had to undergo the baptism of the heavenly tribulation every time they advanced a level. They might die halfway before they could complete the “saber worship.” In that case, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber would have no choice but to change its owner.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber had signed many “reserve digital cultivators” in the contract, and they were all reserve swordmasters.

“Lady Onion’s situation...It was too special. To be honest, I’m still a little confused even though I’m holding the “Eighth Revolution” Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber,” Song Shuhang said.

After saying this, he gently knocked on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, and said, “Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue, it’s always Lady Onion, right?”

Even if there was no information about the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber itself was a divine weapon with a spirit, and it was alive.

“Buzz” Although the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber couldn’t speak, it could transmit its meaning to Song Shuhang through the “saber-man unity” state.

It was Lady Onion!

The Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue had always been Lady Onion, and she was the one who had refined the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber to the eighth rank!

“So, Lady Onion didn’t die,” Song Shuhang said.

As for the “Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue’s information” in the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, it was very likely that Lady Onion didn’t want to leave a record, so she deleted it.

“Buzz” The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber once again transmitted its thoughts and used its answer to prove Song Shuhang’s guess.

As expected, Lady Onion had taken the initiative to delete the records regarding the Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue.

While answering Song Shuhang’s question, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber also used the “saber-man fusion” mode to betray the previous saber master, Lady Onion. It told Song Shuhang that the information regarding the “Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue” had been deleted.

It was as if he had been pulled into the trash bin, and the delete was complete.

However, this didn’t mean that these “messages” had been completely deleted.

Of course, this part of the “information” was not so easy to read.

As the Ninth Cultivator of True Virtue, if Song Shuhang wanted to read this part of the data, he would have to continue to increase the intimacy between him and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber. The state of being one with the saber wasn’t enough, and he needed to go one step further!

“I see. To me...But it’s not a problem!” Song Shuhang laughed.

Then, he stretched out his head and swung his hand. His long hair condensed into more than 20 braided hands, which fell on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber at the same time.

In an instant, a warm light flashed and fell on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

“It’s out! Scumbag Song’s ultimate skill, Cheap Love!” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet couldn’t help but exclaim.

The Saber Nurturing Technique relied on quantity to win, and the love in each saber nurturing technique was so cheap that it made one’s heart ache. However, under the effect of thousands of shots per second, even the cheapest Saber Nurturing Technique could accumulate to an explosive effect!

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber kept making cheerful chirps.

The speed at which the ninth pattern on the saber was unsealed seemed to have stepped on the accelerator and started to accelerate.

The signature of Ninth Cultivator of True Virtue Song One appeared once again.

This time, Pavilion Master Chu finally noticed the signature.

Song One?

“Who are you?”

“Tyrannical Saber Song...Oh, no.” The man in her memory raised his head and gritted his teeth.

“Call me Song One!”

Chapter 2891: Chapter 8.5-Heavenly Dao

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

It was Song One, not Song One.

Although the pronunciation and meaning were the same...However, these were two different ways of writing.

A man’s mouth was a liar.

Pavilion Master Chu would at most believe a little of Slow-Witted Song’s recent secretive words. Among these two points, there was also one point for her friendship and trust.

She knew that Slow-Witted Song had his own difficulties, and there were some things that he couldn’t reveal at the moment...Therefore, Pavilion Master Chu didn’t ask too many questions.

Anyway, it was pointless to ask. There was no way to get the truth out of that guy’s mouth.

In the living spring of the Inner World, Pavilion Master Chu’s main body only revealed half of her face, and her eyes were looking at the sky of the Inner World.

The headquarters of the special world [Heavenly Dao Must Step Down Alliance].

The members of the Alliance were gathered together again today.

“I didn’t expect the current Heavenly Dao to die so easily.” A golden monk sat on the palm of a huge muscular Vajra statue. He clasped his hands together as if he had let go of the obsession in his heart. His entire aura became ethereal. Even the Immortal halo above his head became merciful.

“Congratulations on obtaining your wish, Fellow Daoist.” On the scholarly scholar statue, Daozi held a scroll in his hand and congratulated the golden monk.

The monks of the Titanium Temple had an old grudge with the deceased Heavenly Dao. The Titanium Temple had lost its inheritance in the cultivation world. Even if the Heavenly Dao was not destroyed, the Titanium Temple would not dare to reopen its inheritance.

This was also the reason why the masters of the Titanium Temple had joined the Heavenly Dao Must Step Down Alliance.

Now, the Heavenly Dao had inexplicably collapsed during Tyrannical Song’s tribulation speech, and Tyrannical Song had obtained the special Sage Name ‘Tyrannical Annihilation’. The Heavenly Dao dissipated, and the karma and obsession of the monks of the Titanium Temple disappeared.

Recently, the great master of Titanium Temple, who had been in a good mood, had even taken the initiative to become a ‘boastful troll army’ and bragged about Tyrannical Song. Because the Heavenly Dao had died while Tyrannical Song was giving a speech, the great master of Titanium Temple had a good impression of Tyrannical Song!

He wanted to blow up Tyrannical Song.

Ye Si was sitting on the statue of Empress Cheng Lin.

Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven wasn’t interested in ‘proving the Dao in person.’ He was more interested in nurturing a Wielder of the Will or assisting an Immortal in proving the Dao.

During the last gathering, Daozi was still like,’If you don’t want to vindicate the Dao, then let me do it! I want to vindicate my Dao and become immortal! Why did his stance suddenly change?

“Because I found a better candidate. Someone more suitable than me to vindicate dao.” Daozi held the scripture in his hand and revealed the gentle smile of his eldest senior brother back in the Scholarly Sage’s era.

Tyrannical Song isn’t the reincarnation of anyone, nor is he the backup plan of the Scholarly Sage.” The master of the Titanium Temple said.

The left eye my teacher left behind is in his hands; he has my teacher’s teaching technique, the Impregnating Gaze; he cultivates the special Body of the Buddha technique of my scholarly faction; he helped open up the world of the golden lotus of my scholarly faction; he once summoned my teacher’s obsession as an incarnation to fight against the ruler of the Netherworld in the scholarly faction; and even our most beloved junior sister is now in Tyrannical Song’s body. Isn’t this enough?”

Whether Tyrannical Song was the reincarnation of the Scholarly Sage or not was no longer important. What was important was how the myriad worlds viewed Tyrannical Song.

Daozi wanted to vindicate the Dao to prove that his teacher wasn’t weaker than others and was completely qualified to vindicate the Dao and become immortal.

Therefore, Tyrannical Song was more suitable to vindicate the dao than him!

More importantly, Daozi didn’t say it out loud. To be honest, he wasn’t confident that he could defeat Tyrannical Song.

Even if everyone present knew that Tyrannical Song hadn’t truly become an Immortal, Daozi didn’t have the confidence to win against him.

It wasn’t that Tyrannical Song himself was really powerful, but that his network of human relations was terrifying... There were also many cheats...

“However, Shuhang doesn’t necessarily want to attain immortality. He isn’t passionate about fighting for the seat of the Heavenly Dao, and he’s even a little resistant to it.” Ye Si said at this moment.

Daozi:

Fellow Daoist Daozi, regardless of whether Tyrannical Song vindicates the Dao in the future, before he does... Are you interested in becoming a Heavenly Dao?” At this moment, an illusory shadow appeared and stood on Cheng Lin’s statue.

“Overstepping Heavenly Dao?” Daozi put away the scroll and asked in puzzlement.

” Yes, between the eighth and ninth Wielder of the Will, the 8.5th Wielder of the Will.” The illusory figure said.

With his obsession broken, he entered a temporary state of serenity, making him the calmest in this discussion.

The Heavenly Axiom wasn’t their personal playground. No one could just claim it.

It was the only otherworldly demon in the myriad worlds that retained its consciousness. The curse it sought to break caused the otherworldly demons to lose their intelligence and become wild bosses for the universe’s practitioners.

Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven’s question was direct and insightful.

With the ninth Wielder of the Will on the verge of being born, the reason for creating the 8.5th Wielder of the Will had to be that something crucial needed handling between the eighth and ninth Wielders.

“Fellow Daoists, please, allow me to explain,” began the illusory figure, which soon solidified into the form of a fairy the ‘Fairy of the Dead’ Cheng Goudan.

But now, the Heavenly Dao Ball had collapsed, and the Heavenly Dao was without a master.

If they could create the perfect combination of the Dao of the Heavenly Court and the Heavenly Emperor and trigger the conditions left by the Heavenly Dao Ball, the Heavenly Emperor and the Dao of the Ancient Heavenly City would be absorbed and become part of the Heavenly Dao.

In theory, this would grant a portion of the Heavenly Dao’s authority and possibly some of its eternal nature, making it fitting to call it the 8.5-generation Heavenly Dao.

“But it’s too risky,” Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven said slowly.

No one could guarantee that they wouldn’t lose their will after being absorbed by the Heavenly Dao Ball’s backup plan. If everything were erased and they became part of the Wielder of the Will, the so-called 8.5 Wielder of the Will would be a futile endeavor.

“The method left by the Teacher?” Daozi pondered. “You want to use the Teacher’s method of ‘swallowing a portion of an existence?’”

Using the Scholarly Sage’s method to leave a portion of himself before becoming the 8.5 Wielder of the Will could work. The remaining part would be absorbed and become part of the Heavenly Dao.

This way, even if his consciousness was wiped away, he could still control the 8.5 Wielder of the Will with the remaining part of his existence.

The Scholarly Sage’s method of ‘devouring a portion of an existence’ was highly unconventional. After swallowing it, even after the Heavenly Dao Ball advanced to the Heavenly Dao, it couldn’t directly retrieve the missing part and had to continue proving its immortality with the missing part.

“However, the Teacher’s ability was personal talent. Before the final battle with the previous Wielder of the Will, no one knew of this talent,” Daozi added.

No one had forced the Scholarly Sage to use this talent before. Usually, challengers were easily defeated by the Scholarly Sage. Once the Dimension Portal was opened and the enemy’s tracks locked, the iron fist of knowledge would eliminate over 60% of the enemies.

In the main world, Song Shuhang’s refinement of the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ had reached a crucial stage. The rank nine dao pattern was already 90% complete.

At that moment, a message came from the cultivation chat.

[Zhiyin·Pathogen] Frice Reckless Mad Saber:

“Yes, Senior Thrice Reckless. What’s the matter?” Song Shuhang asked. It was rare for Senior Thrice Reckless to reach out.

“I want to borrow a book from you,” Frice Reckless Mad Saber replied.

“A book? What book?” Song Shuhang was puzzled. What kind of books could he have?

Song Shuhang knew he didn’t have many books on cultivation. Moreover, his collection was not particularly impressive.

Most of what he had, the seniors of the Nine Provinces Number One Group had as well, and they were better stocked.

Could it be that he wanted to borrow the ‘5-Year College Entrance Examination and 3-Year Simulation’ from him?

Chapter 2893: You Are The Senior!

Some of the inner demons in the Dream Realm squeaked, suppressed by the Morality and unable to move. In this domain, only the special Black Panther could move naturally.

Black-skinned Soft Feather: “!!!”

At the side, Fairy Creation quietly looked at Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s posture as he flipped through the book, then turned to look at Song Shuhang, falling silent.

After saying this, Scarlet Heaven Sword kept nudging Song Shuhang’s waist with its hilt, hinting at him.

In the past, it had left the ‘Heart Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword’ with Song Shuhang, and whenever the sword was hit by several hundred rounds of the ? Saber Nurturing Technique ?, the real body of Scarlet Heaven Sword would sense it from afar and relish it. However, nothing beat the sensation of receiving the Saber Nurturing Technique firsthand. Now that it finally had the chance, it couldn’t wait to enjoy the massage.

“Senior, I’ve shifted the position of my kidney. Don’t knock... it’s hollow inside,” Song Shuhang said.

Scarlet Heaven Sword was speechless.

What the heck? Who cares about your kidney? I don’t have any ulterior motives for your waist. What does it have to do with me whether your waist is hollow or not? Moreover, you’re a man with a hollow waist—doesn’t that make you weak?

“Buzz” At this moment, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber chirped softly at Scarlet Heaven Sword, as if greeting a long-lost friend.

“Buzz buzz~ I haven’t seen you in a while... Eh? Wait a minute, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber is actually nearing the ninth transformation?” Scarlet Heaven Sword was suddenly stunned.

It had stayed by Song Shuhang’s side with the inner demon for a long time and had a good understanding of the special Daoist treasure, the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’. Every revolution of the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber needed to be completed by the previous ‘blademaster’ before it was passed on to the next blademaster.

The previous swordmaster, Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue, was a silly onion that Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven had nurtured on a whim. Silly onion completed rank eight, didn’t that mean...that idiot had advanced to the Ninth Stage?

“What the heck! Did Lady Onion awaken?” Scarlet Heaven Sword was stunned. Could it be that silly onion really possessed the appearance of the Heavenly Dao as Scarlet Heaven had predicted?

“In fact, this matter is also related to the disappearance of your inner demon, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword,” Song Shuhang said. “Not long ago, your inner demon, my clone, Lady Onion, and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber all went missing.”

“And then?” Scarlet Heaven Sword asked.

“Currently, only the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber has returned. As you can see, it has already completed the eighth transformation. I’m refining it to complete the last step of the ninth transformation,” Song Shuhang said.

Scarlet Heaven Sword was speechless.

After pondering for a moment, Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “Could it be that something happened to Lady Onion, and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber found a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender to become the ‘Eighth Cultivator of True Virtue,’ and completed the Eighth Revolution?”

“No, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber has confirmed that Lady Onion is the one who completed the ‘Eighth Revolution Sacrificial Refinement,’” Song Shuhang said.

“Heavens. Shuhang, I need to calm down,” Scarlet Heaven Sword said. “It’s best if you let me relax and calm down.”

Song Shuhang was speechless. Senior, if you have something to say, just say it. How tiring is it for me to guess?

Song Shuhang flicked his hair, and it turned into a hundred hands that pressed on Scarlet Heaven Sword’s body at the same time. Some of them landed on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber. The radiance of the ? Blade Nurturing Technique ? exploded. The dazzling light was like a ‘holy light,’ hitting Song Shuhang’s waist and creating a huge ball of holy light, changing the atmosphere.

At times, the addition of holy light would make one imagine even more.

Three seconds later, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber didn’t move at all and didn’t make any sound. They hung on Song Shuhang’s waist silently. The corner of the Great Northern Emperor’s eyes twitched.

The Great Emperor felt that Scarlet Heaven Sword was no longer surnamed Scarlet Heaven, but Song.

Additionally, when Song Shuhang used the ? Saber Nurturing Technique ? and released his immortal elemental energy, the Great Northern Emperor could clearly sense Song Shuhang’s current realm—the Triple-Separated Tribulation Transcender Realm!

Slaying a Triple Separations Tribulation Transcender...this had already surpassed the limits of an ordinary Tribulation Transcender and had entered the level of a weak Immortal!

All of a sudden, the Great Northern Emperor felt like he was choking on a rice cake.

When I was in seclusion, was it really only a few months and not a few thousand years?

Just as he was thinking about it, his Ah Gui’s happy voice came from the side.

“My Lord, you’ve broken out of seclusion!” Senior Turtle called out happily.

The Great Northern Emperor turned his head and looked at his Ah Gui with gratification. Fortunately, his Ah Gui was different from Scarlet Heaven Sword.

“My Lord, while you’re finally out of seclusion, quickly undo the seal on my body!” Senior Turtle spun and landed in the Great Northern Emperor’s arms. “After being suppressed to the Eighth Stage Realm, I feel that I can’t play any role in the midst of so many pendants. I can’t display the strength of a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender. I’m simply dragging you down.”

The Great Northern Emperor: “???”

Pendant? Numerous pendants?

“Don’t worry, the Heavenly Dao has already collapsed. The chaotic period is over. I’ll release your seal now.” The Great Northern Emperor’s expression didn’t change as he said coolly.

He stretched out his hand and pressed it on Ah Gui’s body. He began to undo the realm suppression seal on its body and release its Ninth Grade strength.

“Oh right, my Lord. Which lord are you now?” At the same time that the realm seal on Senior Turtle’s body was removed, it suddenly remembered something.

Other than the Great Northern Emperor that Song Shuhang had revived, there seemed to be another cold Great Northern Emperor in Slow-Witted Song’s golden world.

“Since I know the seal on your back, which one do you think I am?” The Great Northern Emperor revealed a trace of gentleness at the corner of his mouth and gently patted the turtle shell.

“Then... My Lord, have you come into contact with another Great Emperor?” Senior Turtle’s realm began to be released, and it slowly rose back to the Ninth Stage.

“There’s no need to worry about the other ‘me’. After some time, it would fuse with the Dao of the Heavenly Courts and become part of the ‘Completion Plan’. In fact, the other me was never me,” the Great Northern Emperor explained.

That was the old shell that he had shed through ‘death.’

“And my visit this time is also related to this matter,” the Great Northern Emperor looked at Song Shuhang and said. “Shuhang, I came here this time to borrow something from you.”

“Senior Beifang, please speak,” Song Shuhang said.

The Great Northern Emperor had once helped him a great deal. If there was anything he could do to help the Great Emperor, he would do his best to help.

“I want to borrow the fragment of the ancient Heavenly City,” the Great Northern Emperor said. “Don’t worry. Once I’m done using it, I promise to return it in one piece. Moreover, after we succeed, we can give you more fragments of the ancient Heavenly City as compensation for borrowing the fragments of the Heavenly City.”

The Great Northern Emperor’s conditions were very tempting.

However, Song Shuhang was a little embarrassed and said, “Senior, it’s not that I don’t want to lend it...” Instead, after the ancient Heavenly City fragment entered my Inner World, it had already fused with my Inner World. Even if I wanted to lend it, I couldn’t.”

The Great Northern Emperor pinched his chin and fell silent.

He seemed to be secretly communicating with someone.

After a while, the Great Northern Emperor said, “In that case, Shuhang, can you lend us your Inner World to carry out a ritual? When the time comes, we will transfer the fragment of the Heavenly City to your Inner World and complete the ritual. Don’t worry, we won’t interfere with the operation of your Inner World. If necessary, you can limit the scope and authority of the Inner World.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Directly enter my Inner World to carry out the ritual? Send the Heavenly City fragment into my Inner World? Seniors, are you trying to send meat buns into a dog’s mouth?”

Song Shuhang knew that his Inner World had the habit of secretly licking the ‘path of the Heavenly City.’

Chapter 2899: Spare My Dignity!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Song Shuhang didn’t want to deceive the Great Northern Emperor. If the “path of the Heavenly City” that the Great Northern Emperor and the others moved to the fragment of the Heavenly City in his Inner World was affected, their plans might fall apart, and Shuhang would feel uneasy.

“Is that a problem?” The Great Northern Emperor asked, noticing Shuhang’s troubled expression.

“Senior Beifang, it’s not an issue of trust. I’d gladly lend you my Inner World. However, if the fragment of the Heavenly City enters, I might lose something important,” Shuhang explained.

“Lose something? Are you worried that the fragment won’t be able to move out once fused with your Inner World? You don’t have to worry about that,” the Great Northern Emperor reassured. “Once our plan is completed, you can keep that part of the fragment. Only a few key fragments are needed for the Heavenly Court, and you can keep an eye on those.”

“No, that’s not it. My Inner World might absorb the Dao of the Heavenly Emperor from the ancient Heavenly City,” Shuhang clarified.

The Great Northern Emperor was taken aback. “The Dao of the Heavenly Court could also be absorbed?”

“Yes, and if that happens, it could jeopardize the ‘8.5 Heavenly Dao Plan’ that Cheng Lin and Slow-Witted Song mentioned. The plan requires a complete combination of the Dao of the Ancient Heavenly City and the Heavenly Emperor,” Shuhang explained.

“Can you control this?” the Great Northern Emperor asked.

“I can try, but it’s risky. My Inner World might instinctively absorb the Dao of the Heavenly City, like a fire burning a flammable object,” Shuhang said.

The Great Northern Emperor rubbed his forehead in frustration. He fell silent, communicating with someone remotely again. Shuhang waited patiently for his response.

At this moment, Senior White’s gaze fell on a spot behind Shuhang.

“What’s wrong, Senior White?” Shuhang asked.

“What kind of filling do you want?” Senior White asked abruptly.

“Are you still thinking about buns? How about a heart demon filling?” Shuhang joked.

“I wasn’t talking to you,” Senior White replied.

“???” Shuhang was confused.

Senior White handed Shuhang a bun filled with inner demons and then placed another bun with an ‘evil filling’ behind him. A soft voice behind Shuhang thanked Senior White.

It was then that Shuhang noticed a fairy floating in the air, half-lying on his back and fluttering like a flag. She placed her hands on his shoulders and rested her chin on his head while nibbling on the bun.

“Happy New Year in advance, Shuhang,” the fairy said sweetly.

“Happy New Year,” Shuhang replied, feeling an inexplicable closeness to her.

“What gift do you want this year?” Shuhang asked naturally.

“What gift do you want this year?” the fairy echoed, their thoughts seemingly in sync.

“Forget it. I’ll think of a gift myself,” the fairy waved her hand dismissively.

Shuhang smiled faintly and nodded. The fairy was both distressed and happy as she noted, “As your realm increases, our connection deepens. Soon, our thoughts might be completely synchronized.”

“You and I are one,” Shuhang recalled lines he had heard during the ‘Three Corpses Execution’.

“Wrong. You and I are one, but we are not one,” the fairy corrected, taking a big bite of her bun.

Pavilion Master Chu was bewildered by their exchange.

After a while, the Great Northern Emperor finished his remote communication. “Little friend Shuhang, we reached an agreement. Your Inner World can absorb the Dao of the Heavenly City, but during the ritual, please restrain it as much as possible. Is that okay?”

“Senior Beifang, I’ll do my best to help,” Shuhang agreed.

“Then it’s settled. I’ll make some adjustments to the Heavenly City fragment to suit your Inner World,” the Great Northern Emperor said, nodding at his Ah Gui.

“My lord, I need to stay with Tyrannical Song for a while to help find Lady Onion,” Senior Turtle said. “Don’t worry about me. I’ll be safe.”

The Great Northern Emperor left, and soon after, several figures appeared beside Shuhang: Island Master Golden Trigram, Zither Master Phoenix Rites, and Immortal Fairy White Bones.

“Was Senior Beifang here just now?” Immortal Fairy White Bones asked.

“Yes, he was here to borrow the fragment of the Heavenly City,” Shuhang replied.

“Island Master Golden Trigram, I remember you have many fragments of the Heavenly City,” Shuhang added.

“You’re not thinking of taking my fragments, are you?” Island Master Golden Trigram retorted.

“Don’t worry, I’m the new Heavenly Emperor. Show me some respect!” Shuhang joked.

Chapter 2900: She Tricked Me!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

As Island Master Golden Trigram spoke, he accidentally used too much strength while stroking the rabbit, causing it to bark in dissatisfaction.

“Senior Island Master, you’ve misunderstood,” Song Shuhang hurriedly waved his hand and said. “Actually, I don’t have many requirements for the fragments of the Heavenly City. I’m just using them to expand my small world. Now, my Inner World is big enough... Therefore, you don’t have to worry that I’ll aim at your Heavenly City fragment.”

Moreover, Golden Trigram was the second Heavenly Emperor chosen by Da Da Zi, so all the fragments of the Heavenly City belonged to him in name. With Song Shuhang’s personality, it was impossible for him to snatch the treasures of his own people.

Island Master Golden Trigram was speechless. Then, when you suddenly want to expand your small world in the future, will you have designs on my Heavenly Court again?

“Besides, it’s not me who wants to borrow the fragment of the Heavenly City this time. It’s the Great Northern Emperor and his people,” Song Shuhang continued.

“By the way, why did the Great Northern Emperor come here to borrow the fragment of the Heavenly City?” Immortal Fairy White Bones asked curiously. “Could it be that the Great Emperor also wants to reopen the Heavenly Court?”

“The Great Northern Emperor and the other Four Great Emperors are all very strange. I have a feeling that they won’t have any thoughts of rebuilding the Heavenly Court,” Zither Master Fengyi said, her claws tapping thoughtfully.

She had a feeling that before the Heavenly Court was destroyed, the Four Great Emperors, the Ancestral Golden Dragon, and the other elders who built the Heavenly Court with the Celestial Emperor were all mysterious. For example, when the Ancestral Golden Dragon was in the middle stage of the ancient Heavenly City, it only had a name in the Heavenly City and rarely returned.

“Fellow Daoist Beifang and the others have a big plan...” At this moment, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, hanging on Song Shuhang’s waist, suddenly said.

Pavilion Master Chu Daofou, Zither Master Fengyi, Immortal Fairy White Bones, and the others all looked at Scarlet Heaven Sword. They had almost forgotten that Scarlet Heaven Sword had come with the Great Northern Emperor. They had obviously been together before and might have been a small group.

“What plan? Could it be that Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven also participated in this plan?” Immortal Fairy White Bones asked curiously.

“It should be a plan to save myself. I can’t reveal the details... However, someone should be looking for you soon, Fellow Daoist Golden Trigram,” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said.

“As expected, you’re still after the fragment of my Heavenly City?” Island Master Golden Trigram stroked the rabbit. “But no matter who comes, they won’t be able to borrow the fragment of the Heavenly City.”

“Speaking of which... Senior Island Master, now that you have left the mysterious island and have been chatting with me, isn’t your mysterious island now empty? At this time, if someone wants to ‘borrow’ the mysterious island and directly move it away?” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet on the other side of Song Shuhang’s waist couldn’t help but remind him.

Island Master Golden Trigram was speechless. That’s right. The Great Northern Emperor was familiar with Song Shuhang, which was why he came to ‘borrow’ the fragment of the Heavenly City. However, the other teammates of the Great Northern Emperor might not be familiar with him. What if the other party wanted to forcefully borrow the fragment of the Heavenly City and directly targeted his mysterious island?

“I have to go back,” Island Master Golden Trigram rubbed his glabella.

Although the Ancestral Golden Dragon and another fellow daoist proficient in the 36 transformations were still on the island, neither of them was reliable. As expected, it was better for him to go back and guard the mysterious island.

After deciding to leave, Island Master Golden Trigram looked at Song Shuhang—this was the same ‘Senior Song’ who had been a newbie when he first arrived on the mysterious island last year, but had now become a ‘Three Separations Tribulation Transcender’. He had traveled thousands of miles from the mysterious island to meet up with Senior Song because he had been tricked by the previous Heavenly Emperor and wanted to confirm Senior Song’s true identity!

Additionally, some time ago, when he was accepting the inheritance of the Heavenly Emperor and the Dao of the Heavenly City as the new Heavenly Emperor, he had vaguely sensed Senior Song’s forceful interference. At that time, Island Master Golden Trigram, who had received the ‘Dao of the Heavenly City’, vaguely felt that the ‘Senior Song’ that the Heavenly Emperor spoke of gave him a very familiar feeling. Therefore, after fusing with the Dao of the Heavenly City, he immediately came to find Senior Song.

However, he did not expect... This ‘Senior Song’ was actually the newbie who had come to his mysterious island last year. Now, hearing the Heavenly Emperor call him ‘Senior Song’ and ‘Senior Island Master’ again and again, Golden Trigram felt his stomach ache.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, before I leave, I have a question to ask,” said Island Master Golden Trigram.

“Senior Island Master, please ask,” Song Shuhang said.

Island Master Golden Trigram sighed and said, “Why did Heavenly Emperor call you Senior Song? What is your relationship with her?”

“Da Da Zi?” Song Shuhang said.

Island Master Golden Trigram: “???”

“She called me ‘Senior Song’ because she was joking. Of course, it might also be related to Soft Feather,” Song Shuhang said.

“Senior Song is how I address Senior Song,” Soft Feather raised her hand.

Song Shuhang continued, “Da Da Zi’s rebirth this time took over Soft Feather’s ghost spirit... Taking it and not returning it, this kind of behavior must be severely condemned!”

“I see,” Island Master Golden Trigram slightly nodded. No wonder he saw that Soft Feather looked exactly the same as the Heavenly Emperor who had inherited his throne. It turned out that the Heavenly Emperor had taken over this little fairy’s ghost spirit.

“So she was the one who tricked me from beginning to end.” Island Master Golden Trigram’s heart ached.

When he received the inheritance of the Heavenly Emperor, it was easy to explain why he felt so familiar with Tyrannical Song. After all, Song Shuhang had been to the mysterious island before.

After the doubts in his heart were explained to a certain extent, Island Master Golden Trigram cupped his fists at everyone and said, “Then, fairies, fellow Daoists... I have to make a move first. Next time, I’ll come to the mysterious island as a guest.”

Many of the people present were members of the ancient Heavenly City. They were all familiar with each other, so there was no need to be too polite.

After saying that, Golden Trigram began to cast a spell, preparing to open a spatial passageway to return to the mysterious island.

But right at this time, Song Shuhang’s state of enlightenment suddenly changed.

The special state of comprehension after killing the Heavenly Emperor’s Essence Soul finally had a breakthrough after a long period of accumulation and backstage operation. Next to Song Shuhang, the ‘laws’ related to the Heavenly Emperor appeared. There was a portion of the Dao of the Heavenly Court and the Dao of Time that Tiandi Zi was most proficient in. In particular, the Dao of Time resonated with Song Shuhang. The two were highly compatible. Song Shuhang’s ‘secret appraisal technique’ and ‘dreamland’ talent were both related to time.

The data of the Heavenly Emperor’s Dao of Time was analyzed and transformed into simple information that Song Shuhang could understand bit by bit.

When everyone present saw Song Shuhang, their hearts stirred. Due to the influence of the ‘Dao of Time’, when everyone saw Song Shuhang, the scene of their first contact with him began to appear in their minds... After that, he met Song Shuhang, got to know him, and got to know him.

Golden Trigram also turned his head and looked at Song Shuhang. However, the memory that appeared in his mind wasn’t the new Song Shuhang on the mysterious island. In his mind, there was a dusty memory that broke out of its shell. That was the scene when he was still young...
